$('.responsive-menu-pro-button-icon-active').hide();\n          $('.responsive-menu-pro-button-icon-inactive').show();\n\n          if(this.isSingleMenu == 'on'){\n            $(this.container).removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-no-transition');\n          }\n          if(this.animationType != 'fade') {\n            this.setWrapperTranslate();\n          } else {\n            this.fadeMenuIn();\n          }\n          if(this.fadeLinksIn == 'on') {\n            $(\"#responsive-menu-pro > li\").each(function(index) {\n              $(this).show();\n              $(this).animate({opacity: 0}, 0);\n              $(this).delay(100*index).animate({\n                  'margin-left': \"0\",\n                  'opacity': 1\n              }, 500);\n            });\n          }\n          if(this.useSlideEffects == 'on') {\n            var self = this;\n            $('#responsive-menu-pro').promise().done(function(){\n              self.originalHeight = $('#responsive-menu-pro').height();\n              $('#responsive-menu-pro').css({'height': self.originalHeight});\n            });\n          }\n          this.isOpen = true;\n        },\n        closeMenu: function() {\n          $(this.trigger).removeClass(this.activeClass);\n          $('html').removeClass(this.openClass);\n          $('.responsive-menu-pro-button-icon-inactive').hide();\n          $('.responsive-menu-pro-button-icon-active').show();\n          if(this.animationType != 'fade') {\n            this.clearWrapperTranslate();\n          } else {\n            this.fadeMenuOut();\n          }\n          $(\"#responsive-menu-pro > li\").removeAttr('style');\n          this.isOpen = false;\n        },\n        triggerMenu: function() {\n          this.isOpen ? this.closeMenu() : this.openMenu();\n        },\n        backUpSlide: function(backButton) {\n          translate_to = parseInt($('#responsive-menu-pro')[0].style.transform.replace(/^\\D+/g, '')) - 100;\n          $('#responsive-menu-pro').css({'transform': 'translateX(-' + translate_to + '%)'});\n          var previous_submenu_height = this.originalHeight});\n          } else {\n            $('#responsive-menu-pro').css({'height': previous_submenu_height + 'px'});\n          }\n        },\n        triggerSubArrow: function(subarrow) {\n          var sub_menu = $(subarrow).parent().next('.responsive-menu-pro-submenu');\n          var self = this;\n\n          if(this.useSlideEffects == 'on') {\n            $('.responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active').removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active');\n            sub_menu.addClass('responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active');\n            sub_menu.parentsUntil('#responsive-menu-pro').addClass('responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active');\n            current_depth = $(subarrow).parent().parent().parent().data('depth');\n            current_depth = typeof current_depth == 'undefined' ? 1 : current_depth;\n            translation_amount = current_depth * 100;\n            $('#responsive-menu-pro').css({'transform': 'translateX(-' + translation_amount + '%)'});\n            $('#responsive-menu-pro').css({'height': sub_menu.height() + 'px'});\n          } else {\n            if(this.accordion == 'on') {\n              /* Get Top Most Parent and the siblings */\n              var top_siblings = sub_menu.parents('.responsive-menu-pro-item-has-children').last().siblings('.responsive-menu-pro-item-has-children');\n              var first_siblings = sub_menu.parents('.responsive-menu-pro-item-has-children').first().siblings('.responsive-menu-pro-item-has-children');\n              /* Close up just the top level parents to key the rest as it was */\n              top_siblings.children('.responsive-menu-pro-submenu').slideUp(200, 'linear').removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-submenu-open');\n              /* Set each parent arrow to inactive */\n              top_siblings.each(function() {\n                $(this).find('.responsive-menu-pro-subarrow').first().html(self.inactiveArrow);\n                $(this).find('.responsive-menu-pro-subarrow').first().removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active');\n              });\n              /* Now Repeat for the current item siblings */\n              first_siblings.children('.responsive-menu-pro-submenu').slideUp(200, 'linear').removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-submenu-open');\n              first_siblings.each(function() {\n                $(this).find('.responsive-menu-pro-subarrow').first().html(self.inactiveArrow);\n                $(this).find('.responsive-menu-pro-subarrow').first().removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active');\n              });\n            }\n            if(sub_menu.hasClass('responsive-menu-pro-submenu-open')) {\n              sub_menu.slideUp(200, 'linear',function() {\n                $(this).css('display', '');\n              }).removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-submenu-open');\n              $(subarrow).html(this.inactiveArrow);\n              $(subarrow).removeClass('responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active');\n            } else {\n              sub_menu.slideDown(200, 'linear').addClass('responsive-menu-pro-submenu-open');\n              $(subarrow).html(this.activeArrow);\n              $(subarrow).addClass('responsive-menu-pro-subarrow-active');\n            }\n          }\n        },\n        menuHeight: function() {\n          return $(this.container).height();\n        },\n        menuWidth: function() {\n          return $(this.container).width();\n        },\n        wrapperHeight: function() {\n          return $(this.wrapper).height();\n        },\n        setWrapperTranslate: function() {\n          switch(this.animationSide) {\n            case 'left':\n              translate = 'translateX(' + this.menuWidth() + 'px)'; break;\n            case 'right':\n              translate = 'translateX(-' + this.menuWidth() + 'px)'; break;\n            case 'top':\n              translate = 'translateY(' + this.wrapperHeight() + 'px)'; break;\n            case 'bottom':\n              translate = 'translateY(-' + this.menuHeight() + 'px)'; break;\n            }\n            if(this.animationType == 'push') {\n              $(this.pageWrapper).css({'transform':translate});\n              $('html, body').css('overflow-x', 'hidden');\n            }\n            if(this.pushButton == 'on') {\n              $('#responsive-menu-pro-button').css({'transform':translate});\n            }\n        },\n        clearWrapperTranslate: function() {\n          var self = this;\n          if(this.animationType == $(this.container).fadeIn(this.animationSpeed);\n        },\n        fadeMenuOut: function() {\n          $(this.container).fadeOut(this.animationSpeed);\n        },\n        init: function() {\n e.stopPropagation();\n            self.triggerMenu();\n          });\n          $('.responsive-menu-pro-subarrow').on('click', function(e) {\n            e.preventDefault();\n            e.stopPropagation();\n            self.triggerSubArrow(this);\n          });\n          $(window).resize(function() {\n            if($(window).width() > self.breakpoint) {\n == 'on'){\n                $(self.container).addClass('responsive-menu-pro-no-transition');\n              }\n              if($('.responsive-menu-pro-open').length>0){\n                self.setWrapperTranslate();\n              }\n            }\n          });\n          if(this.closeOnLinkClick == 'on') {\n            $(this.linkElement).on('click', function(e) {\n              if($(window).width() < self.breakpoint) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n                /* Fix for when close menu on parent clicks is on */\n                if(self.itemTriggerSubMenu == 'on' && $(this).is('.responsive-menu-pro-item-has-children > ' + self.linkElement)) {\n                  return;\n                }\n                old_href = $(this).attr('href');\n                old_target = typeof $(this).attr('target') == 'undefined' ? '_self' : $(this).attr('target');\n                if(self.isOpen) {\n                  if($(e.target).closest('.responsive-menu-pro-subarrow').length) {\n                    return;\n                  }\n                  if(typeof old_href != 'undefined') {\n                    self.closeMenu();\n                    setTimeout(function() {\n                      window.open(old_href, old_target);\n                    }, self.animationSpeed);\n                  }\n                }\n              }\n            });\n          }\n          if(this.closeOnBodyClick == 'on') {\n            $(document).on('click', 'body', function(e) {\n              if(self.isOpen) {\n                if($(e.target).closest('#responsive-menu-pro-container').length || The <strong><a href=\"/about/leadership/board-of-education/board-members/\">board members</a></strong> represent <a href=\"/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/2014-15_Trustee_Area_Map.pdf\" target=\"_blank\">seven geographic areas</a> and are elected at large for four year terms. For more information about individual board members, click on their photo.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h3><strong>2016-2017 Board Meeting Schedule<br>\n</strong></h3>\n<hr>\n<p>The following is the schedule of regular Board meetings for the 2016-17 school year that was approved by the Board of Education on June 14, 2016. Meetings are held in the board room of the Robert L. Trigg Education Center – 9510 Elk Grove Florin Road, Elk Grove, CA 95624. <strong>Meetings begin at 6 p.m.</strong>, unless otherwise noted, with open session and closed sessions scheduled prior to the regular meetings as necessary.</p>\n<ul>\n<li>July 12, 2016 – 8:30 a.m. – 12:30 p.m.</li>\n<li>August 1, 2016 – 8:30 a.m. – 12:30 p.m.</li>\n<li>August 16, 2016</li>\n<li>September 6 and 20, 2016</li>\n<li>October 4, 2016</li>\n<li>November 1 and 15, 2016</li>\n<li>December 13, 2016</li>\n<li>January 11, 2017 – 8:30 a.m. – 1:30 p.m.<span style=\"color: #155dab;\">*</span></li>\n<li>January 17, 2017</li>\n<li>February 7 and 21, 2017</li>\n<li>March 1, 2017 –&nbsp;8:30 a.m. – 1:30 p.m.<span style=\"color: #155dab;\">*</span></li>\n<li>March 7, 2017</li>\n<li>March 21, 2017</li>\n<li>April 4 and 18, 2017</li>\n<li>May 2 and 16, 2017</li>\n<li>June 13 and 27, 2017</li>\n</ul>\n<p><strong><span style=\"color: #155dab;\">*</span> Special Board Meeting</strong></p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h3>Board Meeting Agendas</h3>\n<hr>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-615\" src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/AO_logo2.png\" alt=\"AO_logo2\" width=\"186\" height=\"32\"><br>\nThe Elk Grove Unified School District uses the Agenda Online system. This Web-based application allows you to access board meeting information including agendas, supporting documents and minutes, from any computer that has Internet access.<br>\n<strong><br>\n<span class=\"wp-svg-globe globe\"></span> <a href=\"https://agendaonline.net/public/Agency.aspx?PublicAgencyID=24&amp;AgencyTypeID=1\" target=\"_blank\">View EGUSD Board meeting agendas</a>*</strong></p>\n<p>*Please note: Finalized agendas will be available 72 hours prior to the meeting date/time.</p>\n<p><strong><span class=\"wp-svg-arrow-right-3 2015)</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h3>Board Policies</h3>\n<hr>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-1657\" src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/GamutOnline2.png\" alt=\"Gamut Online Logo\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">Initiatives</span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>In Elk Grove Unified, our number one priority is to help every student learn in every classroom, in every subject, every day, and to prepare them to be college and career ready. To support that mission, the district offers several programs and services that align to four strategic goals which are centered on providing quality instruction, developing assessments and analysis for action, promoting wellness and engaging families and the community. For continuous improvement, in addition to promoting leadership development, professional learning, technology infrastructure, systems of communication, program implementation, research-based practices, and cultural competence the district takes steps to implement key initiatives to address specific needs.</p>\n<ul>\n<li>Improving <a href=\"/about/district/initiatives/improving-attendance/\">Attendance and Addressing Chronic Absenteeism</a></li>\n<li>Keeping Students Technically Literate Through <a href=\"http://blogs.egusd.net/digitalcitizenship/\" target=\"_blank\">Digital Citizenship and Internet Safety</a></li>\n<li>Preparing Students For College and Career with a <a href=\"/academics/college-and-career-readiness/\">Graduate Profile</a></li>\n<li>Recognizing the Link Between <a href=\"/about/district/district-initiatives/healthy-body-healthy-mind-healthy-learning/\">Healthy Body, Healthy Mind and Healthy Learning</a></li>\n<li>Informing About Modernization and Maintenance Needs – <a href=\"/about/divisions-departments/facilities-and-planning/\">Measure M</a></li>\n<li>Helping Students <a href=\"/about/district/initiatives/on-grade-level-reading/\">Read On Grade Level</a></li>\n<li>Engaging <a href=\"/students-families/family-and-community-engagement-face/\">Families and the Community</a> to Support Students</li>\n</ul>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel\" id=\"lcap-tab\" data-vc-content=\".vc_tta-panel-body\"><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-heading\"><h4 class=\"vc_tta-panel-title\"><a href=\"#lcap-tab\" data-vc-accordion=\"\" data-vc-container=\".vc_tta-container\"><span class=\"vc_tta-title-text\">LCFF/LCAP</span></a></h4></div><div class=\"vc_tta-panel-body\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<h3><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-5975\" src=\"http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/LCFF-LCAP-notagline-300x84.png\" alt=\"LCFF-LCAP Logo\" width=\"200\" height=\"56\" srcset=\"http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/LCFF-LCAP-notagline-300x84.png 300w, http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/LCFF-LCAP-notagline.png 768w, http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/LCFF-LCAP-notagline-700x197.png 700w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px\"></h3>\n<h3>Local Control Funding Formula (LCFF) /Local Control Accountability Plan (LCAP)</h3>\n<p>The LCFF and LCAP represent dramatic changes in the way that the State of California funds public education, and EGUSD is committed to open communication with all stakeholders to ensure that our yearly LCAP clarifies how programs and services will measurably improve in proportion to increased LCFF funding.</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/FINAL_LCAP_BOARD_APPROVED_6-28-16-sqbo1i.pdf\" target=\"_blank\"><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-5868 size-full\" src=\"http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/EGUSD_LCAP-1yak2is.jpg\" sizes=\"(max-width: 361px) 100vw, 361px\" srcset=\"http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/EGUSD_LCAP-1yak2is.jpg 361w, http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/EGUSD_LCAP-1yak2is-300x224.jpg 300w\" alt=\"2016-2019 EGUSD Local Control Accountability Plan\" width=\"361\" height=\"270\"></a></p>\n<h3>EGUSD’s 2016-2019 Adopted&nbsp;LCAP</h3>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/FINAL_LCAP_BOARD_APPROVED_6-28-16-sqbo1i.pdf\" target=\"_blank\">English</a> | <a \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-5517\" src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/freshlogo2.png\" alt=\"Food and Nutrition Services Logo\" width=\"250\" height=\"113\"><br>\nMeals served at school meet state and federal requirements based on the USDA Dietary Guidelines. &nbsp;All meals are prepared and served by qualified child nutrition professionals. &nbsp;We provide students with access to a variety of fresh and appealing foods that meet the health and nutrition needs of students.</p>\n<p>When students have eaten, they are better able to concentrate and participate&nbsp;in the classroom. &nbsp;Well nourished students make better learners.</p>\n<p><span class=\"wp-svg-globe globe\"></span>&nbsp;<a href=\"http://blogs.egusd.net/fns/meals/menusnutrition-info/elementary/\" target=\"_blank\">Elementary Breakfast and Lunch Menu/Nutrition&nbsp;Information<br>\n</a><span class=\"wp-svg-globe globe\"></span> <a href=\"http://blogs.egusd.net/fns/meals/menusnutrition-info/middle-schoolhigh-school/\" target=\"_blank\">Middle School/High School Menu/Nutritional Information</a><br>\n<span class=\"wp-svg-globe globe\"></span> <a href=\"http://blogs.egusd.net/fns/meals/menusnutrition-info/elementary/\" target=\"_blank\">Snack Carbohydrates</a><br>\n<span class=\"wp-svg-globe globe\"></span> <a href=\"http://blogs.egusd.net/fns/meals/menusnutrition-info/elementary/\" target=\"_blank\">Supper Carbohydrates<br>\n</a></p>\n<hr>\n<p>Free and Reduced Price Meals are available, under the National School Lunch Program (NSLP), to all families who believe they may qualify.&nbsp;There are two ways to apply.</p>\n<ol>\n<li>Complete a Free and Reduced Price Meal Application online.&nbsp;The online application allows you to apply online in the comfort and privacy of your home.&nbsp;It is convenient, safe, secure and available anytime.</li>\n<li>Complete a paper Free and Reduced Price Meal Application form.&nbsp;Paper forms can be obtained at any school office within the district or at the Food &amp; Nutrition Services office and returned to any school office, cafeteria or the Elk Grove Unified Food &amp; Nutrition Services office at 8389 Gerber Road, Sacramento, CA 95828.<br>\n<a href=\"https://freeandreducedmeals.com/lfserver/EGUSD_FRAAPP_ENG_16-17\" target=\"_blank\"><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-5513 size-full\" src=\"/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/FNS_meal_app.png\" alt=\"2016-2017 Meal Application Logo - Click to Apply\" width=\"175\" height=\"175\" srcset=\"http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/FNS_meal_app.png 175w, http://www.egusd.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/FNS_meal_app-150x150.png 150w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 175px) 100vw, 175px\"></a></li>\n</ol>\n<p><strong><span class=\"wp-svg-globe globe\"></span>&nbsp;<a href=\"https://freeandreducedmeals.com/lfserver/EGUSD_FRAAPP_ENG_16-17\" target=\"_blank\">2016-2017 online meal application</a></strong></p>\n<hr>\n<p>If you have any questions about the school breakfast/lunch menus or would like more information about Free and Reduced Price Meals or the application process, please contact:<br>\n<strong><br>\nFood &amp;&nbsp;Nutrition Services</strong><br>\n<span class=\"wp-svg-phone phone\"></span> (916) 686-7735<br>\n<span
